Active Hero's Echo
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Elemental Slash
Master Level 1
Description Attack enemies in front of you with pure, primal energy.
Level 1 MP Cost: 0, Damage: 130%, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 3


Active Imperial Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to the Empress using Shinsoo's power.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, return to Ereve immediately.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Passive Elemental Harmony
Master Level 1
Description Use the harmony of nature to build affinity for an element of your choosing.
Level 1 Intelligence increases 1 for every 2 levels the character gains


Passive Elemental Expert
Master Level 1
Description Become an expert of the elements to increase Attack Power and Magic ATT.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +10%


Passive Elemental Shift
Master Level 1
Description Jump in any direction except down by pressing a direction key and jump in midair.
Level 1 MP Cost: 4, jumps further in the appropriate direction

Passive Cygnus Blessing (Magician)
Master Level 10
Description Blessings from an awakened Empress Cygnus protect you from harm.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 5 times, once for each unique Cygnus Knights job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +7, Abnormal Status Resistance: +1, All Elemental Resistance: +1%
10 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +25, Abnormal Status Resistance: +15, All Elemental Resistance: +15%

Master Level 5
Description Jump into the air and disappear in a burst of flames, reappearing some distance ahead. Permanently raises your Defense, Jump, and Max Speed.

Active Orbital Explosion
Master Level 10
Description Harness and release the essence of the flame.
When Orbital Flame, Phoenix Drive, Orbital Inferno, Inferno Sphere, or Eternity land a certain number of times, the next attack will be an additional fire-attribute flame energy hit.
The flame energy hits are unaffected by enemy damage reflection skills.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 MP Cost: 10
When Orbital Flame, Phoenix Drive, Orbital Inferno, Inferno Sphere, or Eternity lands 10 times, the next Orbital Flame type skill, Inferno Sphere, or Eternity attack will be an additional hit dealing 28% damage 3 times.
10 MP Cost: 13
When Orbital Flame, Phoenix Drive, Orbital Inferno, Inferno Sphere, or Eternity lands 10 times, the next Orbital Flame type skill, Inferno Sphere, or Eternity attack will be an additional hit dealing 55% damage 3 times.

Active Flashfire
Master Level 5
Description Leave a trail of fire from your current location. While the trail remains, you can use Flashfire again to teleport back to your original position.
Use the skill with the down key to leave a trail of fire again.
Level 1 MP Cost: 41, Leave a trail of fire that lasts 20 sec.
Use skill the again to teleport to the trail's location. Teleport Cooldown: 2 sec.
Use the skill again and hold the down key to replace the trail. Once replaced, you cannot replace the trail again for 1 sec.
5 MP Cost: 45, Leave a trail of fire that lasts 100 sec.
Use skill the again to teleport to the trail's location. Teleport Cooldown: 2 sec.
Use the skill again and hold the down key to replace the trail. Once replaced, you cannot replace the trail again for 1 sec.

Active Controlled Burn
Master Level 9
Description Recover from the heat of battle and convert your internal flame to MP.
Absorb the enemy's MP when attacking with flame Magic skills. Absorption efficiency is reduced against bosses, resulting in less MP gained.
Level 1 Recovers 44% of your MP upon casting.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effects: MP Absorb Chance: 6%, Amount Absorbed: 3% of Max MP
Amount Absored: 0% of the boss's Max MP]
9 Recovers 100% of your MP upon casting.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effects: MP Absorb Chance: 22%, Amount Absorbed: 7% of Max MP
Amount Absored: 4% of the boss's Max MP]

Passive Final Orbital Flame
Master Level 30
Description Borrow power from the mischievous Flame Fox to launch a flame forward that doesn't return. Up to 4 flames can be active at the same time, and using it a certain number of times allows the use of enhanced Orbital Flame. Use the arrow keys to direct.
Fox Mischief debuff activates when it lands a certain number of times.
When Fox Mischief stacks 5 times, you can hit with Towering Inferno Fox Mode and make it explode. This is a fire attack.
Required Skill: Grand Orbital Flame Lv. 20
Level 1 MP Cost: 37, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 396%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec
30 MP Cost: 43, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 570%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec
31 MP Cost: 43, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 576%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec
32 MP Cost: 43, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 582%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec

Passive Towering Inferno
Master Level 30
Description The Flame Fox temporarily returns to a state of pure fire and flies in front. Enemies with 5 stacks of Fox Mischief will take greater damage.
Towering Inferno Fox Mode cooldown decreases every time your attack lands.
Using it while pressing the down arrow key activates Towering Inferno Lion Mode. This is a fire attack. Can be used only when Flame Fox is summoned.

Active Fires of Creation
Master Level 30
Description Summons the very essence of fire itself. Using this skill will call forth Blazing Lion. Using it with Down pressed will call forth Flame Fox.
While the summoning is in effect, your MP costs increase, but your attacks ignore some enemy defense.
Attack varies upon using Orbital Flame or Towering Inferno based on the Fire Essence summoned.
Level 1 required to learn Towering Inferno.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, Duration: 300, MP Consumption: +105%, Ignore Defense: +1%
30 MP Cost: 115, Duration: 300, MP Consumption: +105%, Ignore Defense: +30%
31 MP Cost: 115, Duration: 300, MP Consumption: +105%, Ignore Defense: +31%
32 MP Cost: 116, Duration: 300, MP Consumption: +105%, Ignore Defense: +32%

Active Decent Combat Orders
Master Level 25
Description Temporarily increases all of your skill levels. Only 4th Job Skills can be increased beyond master level while other skills can only be increased to master level.
Exceptions: Some special skills, Beginner Skills, Combat Orders, Decent Combat Orders, Hyper Skills, and 5th Job Skills cannot be increased.
Does not stack with Combat Orders.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of Max HP, Duration: 183 sec, All Skills: +1
Cooldown: 180 sec
[Passive Effect - Abnormal Status Resistance: +1]

Cooldown: 180 sec
[Passive Effect - Abnormal Status Resistance: +5]

Cooldown: 180 sec

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]

If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]
Show/hide all levels
Active True Arachnid Reflection
Master Level 25
Description The collapsing space between the Mirror World and reality become linked with Will's Erda, causing the spider within the mirror to temporarily materialize in reality.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP
Spatial Collapse - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 15, Once complete, summons True Arachnid Reflection.
True Arachnid Reflection - Duration: 50 sec, Goes into attack mode at set intervals. During attack mode, uses spider legs 10 times to deal 182% damage 8 times. If the spider legs attack one target 5 consecutive times, attack mode will end immediately. 3 sec cooldown after attack mode ends.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Cooldown: 250 sec

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 41
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec
25 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 900%, Number of Attacks: 65
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec
30 MP Cost: 500, Damage: 990%, Number of Attacks: 70
Spearmen disappear when the number of attacks is reached, they move a certain distance, or after a certain duration. Activate the skill again to change their direction.
Cooldown: 30 sec

Active Ethereal Form
Master Level 25
Description Moves you to a different dimension to reduce the damage you take. Use the skill again to return. While in Ethereal Form, you cannot use other skills.
Level 1 HP Cost: 1000, Duration: 3 sec. Grants Knockback Immunity. Situations that would normally cause you to take damage instead reduce your MP by 9910. If this would reduce your MP below 0, you will instead take normal HP damage. If your job does not utilize MP, you will instead lose 2470 HP.
Cooldown: 60 sec.
25 HP Cost: 1000, Duration: 3 sec. Grants Knockback Immunity. Situations that would normally cause you to take damage instead reduce your MP by 7750. If this would reduce your MP below 0, you will instead take normal HP damage. If your job does not utilize MP, you will instead lose 1750 HP.
Cooldown: 60 sec.
30 HP Cost: 1000, Duration: 3 sec. Grants Knockback Immunity. Situations that would normally cause you to take damage instead reduce your MP by 7300. If this would reduce your MP below 0, you will instead take normal HP damage. If your job does not utilize MP, you will instead lose 1600 HP.
Cooldown: 60 sec.

Active Savage Flame
Master Level 25
Description Unleash the true might of the Essence of Fire. Only usable while Fires of Creation is active. Attack varies based on the Fire Essence summoned. Using it while pressing the down arrow key will activate an attack that matches a Fire Essence that isn't summoned.
This skill consumes all the flames, boosting its attack power in proportion to the number of flames consumed. It's a fire-attribute attack.
Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 Passive Effects: Gain 1 Flame Charge when a normal enemy is hit 1 times, boss is hit 25 times (stacks 1 time upon landing the skill) or a boss is defeated 1 times with Blaze Wizard's direct skill attack, up to 6 flames.
Active Effect - MP Cost: 500, Flame Cost: 2+ charges, Cooldown: 20 sec.
[Blazing Lion]: Activates explosion 12 times, hitting up to 15 enemies for 312% damage. Flames remain for 18 sec, triggering explosions against up to 5 enemies who are caught in the flames. Each explosion attacks up to 3 enemies for 312% damage 5 times. Each enemy can trigger an explosion up to 5 times.
Increases Final Damage of all Blazing Lion attacks by 35% for every Flame Charge over the minimum cost.
[Flame Fox]: Maintained up to 5 sec. Creates 8 foxfires that target the boss with the highest HP first and strike 8 enemies within range. Each foxfire deals 394% damage and can regenerate up to 7 times.
Regenerates 2 more time for each 1 Flame Charge over the minimum cost.
25 Passive Effects: Gain 1 Flame Charge when a normal enemy is hit 1 times, boss is hit 25 times (stacks 1 time upon landing the skill) or a boss is defeated 1 times with Blaze Wizard's direct skill attack, up to 6 flames.
Active Effect - MP Cost: 500, Flame Cost: 2+ charges, Cooldown: 20 sec.
[Blazing Lion]: Activates explosion 12 times, hitting up to 15 enemies for 600% damage. Flames remain for 18 sec, triggering explosions against up to 5 enemies who are caught in the flames. Each explosion attacks up to 3 enemies for 600% damage 5 times. Each enemy can trigger an explosion up to 5 times.
Increases Final Damage of all Blazing Lion attacks by 35% for every Flame Charge over the minimum cost.
[Flame Fox]: Maintained up to 5 sec. Creates 8 foxfires that target the boss with the highest HP first and strike 8 enemies within range. Each foxfire deals 730% damage and can regenerate up to 7 times.
Regenerates 2 more time for each 1 Flame Charge over the minimum cost.

Active Salamander Mischief
Master Level 25
Description Summon the fire of a playful salamander spirit.
Salamander tracks a nearby enemy to attack when a direct skill attack by Blaze Wizard hits. In a single action, it either consumes all of the number of attacks or returns to the summoner's location when it strays too far.
Obtain Ember every time Salamander's attack hits, and Salamander's attack becomes stronger in proportion. You can get a Magic ATT increase buff in return for the Ember when Salamander disappears.
Unaffected by attack reflection, and prioritizes boss with highest Max HP. It's a fire-attribute attack.
Level 1 MP Cost: 250, Salamander Summon Duration: 60 sec, Damage: 157%, Enemies Hit: 1, Number of Attacks: 7. In a single action, consumes 100 MP and attacks by bouncing up to 12 times.
Obtain Ember every time Salamander's attack hits. Final Damage of Salamander's attack increases by 1% for every 1 Ember. Up to 16 Ember can be obtained.
When Salamander disappears, Magic ATT increases by 15 for 30 sec, and Magic ATT additionally increases by 2 for every 1 Ember.
Cooldown: 90 sec
25 MP Cost: 250, Salamander Summon Duration: 60 sec, Damage: 325%, Enemies Hit: 1, Number of Attacks: 7. In a single action, consumes 100 MP and attacks by bouncing up to 12 times.
Obtain Ember every time Salamander's attack hits. Final Damage of Salamander's attack increases by 1% for every 1 Ember. Up to 40 Ember can be obtained.
When Salamander disappears, Magic ATT increases by 15 for 30 sec, and Magic ATT additionally increases by 2 for every 1 Ember.
Cooldown: 90 sec

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Active Eternity
Master Level 30
Description The phoenix that rules over the cycle of life and death manifests, bringing death to all. The phoenix creates a Flame of the Cycle on the ground for a certain period of time.

Lv. 10: Ignore Defense +20%
Lv. 20: Boss Damage +20%
Lv. 30: Ignore Defense +30% and Boss Damage +30%

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Show/hide all levels
Active HEXA Orbital Flame [2]
Master Level 30
Description Mastering fire magic enhances Orbital Flame's damage.
Up to 4 can be unleashed at the same time, and using it a certain number of times allows use of an enhanced Orbital Flame.
Powerful magic forms a huge flame where the Orbital Flame passed by at regular intervals. It is a fire-attribute attack.
Required SKill: Orbital Flame IV Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 45, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 411%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Upon using 3 times, the next attack activates the enhanced HEXA Orbital Flame, which creates a flame 4 times that attacks up to 6 enemies for 446% damage 9 times every 15 seconds
30 MP Cost: 45, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 440%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +50%
Upon using 3 times, the next attack activates the enhanced HEXA Orbital Flame, which creates a flame 4 times that attacks up to 6 enemies for 620% damage 9 times every 15 seconds

Active HEXA Orbital Flame [4]
Master Level 30
Description Borrows power from the more powerful Flame Fox to launch a flame in front that doesn't return. Up to 4 flames can be used at the same time, and using it a certain number of times allows use of an enhanced Orbital Flame. Use the arrow keys to direct.
Fox Mischief debuff activates when it lands a certain number of times, and reduces Elemental Resistance.
When Fox Mischief stacks 5 times, you can hit with Towering Inferno - Fox and make it explode. Party members cannot stack the effect with Dawn Warrior's <True Sight - Enhanced>'s effect or Battle Mage's <Weakening Aura - Elemental Decrease>'s Elemental Resistance decrease effect, but Blaze Wizard itself can stack the effects.
A huge flame is formed where the Orbital Flame passed by at regular intervals with powerful magic. It's a fire-attribute attack.
Required Skill: Final Orbital Flame Lv. 30
Level 1 MP Cost: 45, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 731%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing, Enemy Elemental Resistance: -10%. Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec
Every 15 seconds, creates flame 4 times that attack up to 6 enemies with 446% damage 9 times at regular intervals
30 MP Cost: 45, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 760%, Number of Attacks: 2
Upon landing, Enemy Elemental Resistance: -10%. Upon landing 10 times, Fox Mischief Debuff Duration: 20 sec
Every 15 seconds, creates flame 4 times that attack up to 6 enemies with 620% damage 9 times at regular intervals

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
